                                 <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">$$\begin{equation}\sigma = L/RS\end{equation}$$</annotation>
                              </semantics></math></span><span class="inline-equation__label">(2)</span></div>where <i>S</i>, <i>R</i>, and <i>L</i> represent the area of the stainless steel, the impedance of the SS//MCE//SS cell, and the thickness of the prepared electrolyte membranes, respectively.</div>
                  
                  <div class="paragraph-element">The corresponding activation energy of the MCE was accurately fitted based on the Arrhenius equation, represented by Formula&nbsp;3

                     <div class="inline-equation" id="adfm202314288-disp-0003"><span class="inline-equation__construct"><!--FIGURE-->
                           <span class="fallback__mathEquation" data-altimg="/cms/asset/e2b55332-a3d7-4859-b38e-4e6519f30399/adfm202314288-math-0008.png"></span><math altimg="urn:x-wiley:1616301X:media:adfm202314288:adfm202314288-math-0008" display="block" location="graphic/adfm202314288-math-0008.png">
                              <semantics>
                                 <mrow>
                                    <mfrac>
                                       <mi>T</mi>
                                       <mrow>
                                          <mi>R</mi>
                                          <mi>ct</mi>
                                       </mrow>
                                    </mfrac>
                                    <mo linebreak="badbreak">=</mo>
                                    <mi>A</mi>
                                    <mi>e</mi>
                                    <mi>x</mi>
                                    <mi>p</mi>
                                    <mfenced close=")" open="(" separators="">
                                       <mfrac>
                                          <mrow>
                                             <mi>E</mi>
                                             <mi mathvariant="normal">a</mi>
                                          </mrow>
                                          <mrow>
                                             <mi>R</mi>
                                             <mi>T</mi>
                                          </mrow>
                                       </mfrac>
                                    </mfenced>
                                 </mrow>
                                 <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">$$\begin{equation}\frac{T}{{R{\mathrm{ct}}}} = Aexp\left( {\frac{{E{\mathrm{a}}}}{{RT}}} \right)\end{equation}$$</annotation>
                              </semantics></math></span><span class="inline-equation__label">(3)</span></div>where <i>T</i>, <i>R</i><sub>ct</sub>, <i>A</i>, <i>E</i><sub>a</sub>, and <i>R</i> are the absolute temperature, interfacial transfer resistance, pre-exponential factor, activation energy, and gas constant, respectively.</div>
                  
                  <div class="paragraph-element">The Na<sup>+</sup> transference number of the MCE was measured with Na//MCE//Na symmetric battery by the chronoamperometry method combining the EIS and direct-current (DC) polarization (10&nbsp;mV), which was calculated by Formula&nbsp;4

                     <div class="inline-equation" id="adfm202314288-disp-0004"><span class="inline-equation__construct"><!--FIGURE-->
                           <span class="fallback__mathEquation" data-altimg="/cms/asset/86ab086f-1b3d-4926-bbd9-78b410d969c9/adfm202314288-math-0009.png"></span><math altimg="urn:x-wiley:1616301X:media:adfm202314288:adfm202314288-math-0009" display="block" location="graphic/adfm202314288-math-0009.png">
                              <semantics>
                                 <mrow>
                                    <mi>t</mi>
                                    <mo linebreak="badbreak">=</mo>
                                    <mfrac>
                                       <mrow>
                                          <msub>
                                             <mi>I</mi>
                                             <mi mathvariant="normal">s</mi>
                                          </msub>
                                          <mfenced close=")" open="(" separators="">
                                             <mrow>
                                                <mi mathvariant="normal">Δ</mi>
                                                <mi>V</mi>
                                                <mo>−</mo>
                                                <msub>
                                                   <mi>I</mi>
                                                   <mi mathvariant="normal">o</mi>
                                                </msub>
                                                <msub>
                                                   <mi>R</mi>
                                                   <mi mathvariant="normal">o</mi>
                                                </msub>
                                             </mrow>
                                          </mfenced>
                                       </mrow>
                                       <mrow>
                                          <msub>
                                             <mi>I</mi>
                                             <mi mathvariant="normal">o</mi>
                                          </msub>
                                          <mfenced close=")" open="(" separators="">
                                             <mrow>
                                                <mi mathvariant="normal">Δ</mi>
                                                <mi>V</mi>
                                                <mo>−</mo>
                                                <msub>
                                                   <mi>I</mi>
                                                   <mi mathvariant="normal">s</mi>
                                                </msub>
                                                <msub>
                                                   <mi>R</mi>
                                                   <mi mathvariant="normal">s</mi>
                                                </msub>
                                             </mrow>
                                          </mfenced>
                                       </mrow>
                                    </mfrac>
                                    <mspace width="0.33em"></mspace>
                                 </mrow>
                                 <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">$$\begin{equation}t = \frac{{{{I}_{\mathrm{s}}}\left( {{{\Delta}}V - {{I}_{\mathrm{o}}}{{R}_{\mathrm{o}}}} \right)}}{{{{I}_{\mathrm{o}}}\left( {{{\Delta}}V - {{I}_{\mathrm{s}}}{{R}_{\mathrm{s}}}} \right)}}\ \end{equation}$$</annotation>
                              </semantics></math></span><span class="inline-equation__label">(4)</span></div>where the <i>I</i><sub>0</sub>, <i>I</i><sub>S</sub>, <i>R</i><sub>0</sub>, and <i>R</i><sub>S</sub> represent the initial current, steady-state current, and the resistance before and after polarization, respectively.</div>
                  
                  <p>The polarization voltage Δ<i>V</i> was 10&nbsp;mV. The interface impedance of the MCEs was tested by EIS with an amplitude of 0.01&nbsp;V and a frequency of 0.01–10<sup>6</sup> Hz.</p>
                  
                  <p>The ESW of this electrolyte was tested by LSV of SS//MCE//Na battery in a range of 1–6&nbsp;V at a scan rate of 0.1&nbsp;mV S<sup>−1</sup>.</p>
                  </section>
               
               <section class="article-section__sub-content" id="adfm202314288-sec-0190">
                  
                  <h4 class="article-section__sub-title section4" id="adfm202314288-sec-0190-title"> Morphology and Structure Characterization</h4>
                  
                  <p>The XRD patterns were performed on the Rigaku SmartLab with a Cu K<sub>α</sub> radiation source. The SEM images and energy dispersive X-ray (EDX) were obtained using JEOL, JSM-7900F scanning electron microscope at an acceleration voltage of 15&nbsp;kV. Nitrogen-sorption studies were performed at 77 K up to 1&nbsp;bar with an ASAP 2020 HD88 (Micromeritics). Before the sorption measurements, the samples were activated under 150 °C for 24&nbsp;h. TGA was carried out using a simultaneous PerkinElmer STA 8000 at a heating rate of 5 °C min<sup>−1</sup> under air atmosphere. XPS measurement was performed on a Thermo Scientific K-Alpha system in vacuum (≈3 × 10<sup>−7</sup>&nbsp;mbar) with Al K<sub>α</sub> source at 12&nbsp;kV and 6&nbsp;mA. The monochromator was equipped with an Ar<sup>+</sup> ion sputtering gun, which adjusted different etching times for samples. The HR-TEM images were acquired in a TEM (FEI, Talos F200X G2) at 200&nbsp;kV. The FT-IR information was characterized by Bruker Tensor II Sample Compartment RT-DLaTGS. Raman spectroscopy was collected from Thermo-Fisher Scientific, excitation S4 wavelength, 532&nbsp;nm. The solid-state NMR was acquired in an NMR (Bruker, 400&nbsp;MHz Digital Solid-State NMR Spectrometer).</p>
                  </section>
               
               <section class="article-section__sub-content" id="adfm202314288-sec-0200">
                  
                  <h4 class="article-section__sub-title section4" id="adfm202314288-sec-0200-title"> Computational Details</h4>
                  
                  <p>All the calculations in this work were performed using the VASP code.<sup>[</sup><span><sup><a href="#adfm202314288-bib-0025" class="bibLink tab-link" id="adfm202314288-bib-0025_R_d104888562e1611" data-tab="pane-pcw-references" aria-label="Reference 25 - Phys. Rev. B Phys. Rev. B">25</a></sup></span><sup>]</sup> The valence electron and core-ion interactions were described using the projected augmented wave (PAW),<sup>[</sup><span><sup><a href="#adfm202314288-bib-0026" class="bibLink tab-link" id="adfm202314288-bib-0026_R_d104888562e1616" data-tab="pane-pcw-references" aria-label="Reference 26 - Phys. Rev. B Phys. Rev. B">26</a></sup></span><sup>]</sup> and the electron exchange and correlation energies were calculated using the GGA/PBE exchange-correlation functional.<sup>[</sup><span><sup><a href="#adfm202314288-bib-0027" class="bibLink tab-link" id="adfm202314288-bib-0027_R_d104888562e1621" data-tab="pane-pcw-references" aria-label="Reference 27 - Phys. Rev. Lett.">27</a></sup></span><sup>]</sup> A cutoff energy of 450&nbsp;eV was applied to the plane wave basis expansion. The Na-ion self-diffusion was calculated on a 1 × 1 × 2 supercell with 324 atoms using the climbing image nudged elastic band (CI-NEB) method<sup>[</sup><span><sup><a href="#adfm202314288-bib-0028" class="bibLink tab-link" id="adfm202314288-bib-0028_R_d104888562e1627" data-tab="pane-pcw-references" aria-label="Reference 28 - J. Chem. Phys. J. Chem. Phys.">28</a></sup></span><sup>]</sup> to seek the saddle points and minimum energy paths. Accordingly, a 1 × 1 × 3 Monkhorst–Pack k-point grid was used for the integration over the first Brillouin zone. The lattice parameters and ionic positions were fully relaxed until the total energies and ionic forces were less than 10<sup>−5</sup>&nbsp;eV and 0.02&nbsp;eV Å<sup>−1</sup>, respectively.</p>
                  </section>
               </section>
            </section>
         </section>
